     <p> A goat skull sits upon a large, flat rock at the peak of the mountain, its hollow eyes gazing out across the valley below. </p>   <p> <a class="btn-icon" onclick="javascript:window.app.reroll('3vsxpsrJ');"><i class="fa fa-dice"></i></a> Music drifts near the base of the tallest mountain.  A warm, honeyed melody inviting you to listen a while. Following the music to its source you find Hrotho, a terrified bard surrounded by sleeping monsters (from the random encounters table). He stares at you in desperation, trapped by his own lullaby and unable to escape. <p> <strong>Hrotho of Balaal</strong>. engravings, can be found wedged near the base of a steep cliff.  <p> There's a <a class="btn-spawn-dice" data-dice='1d6' onclick="javascript:window.app.spawn_dice('1d6');"><strong>1-in-6</strong></a> chance to find a secret door leading inside the artifact and a successful <strong>INT</strong> check will allow using a contraption inside it. </p> <p> If used, the object will magically levitate and
